Validation\nand archival of radiation\nmeasureme.nts\nmade\nby ERBE\ninstruments\nduring this second year of operation\nwere completed\niz_\n,luly 1991.\nThis period includes\nthe only time, November\n1986 thTvugh January 1987, during which all ERBE instruments\naboard the ERBS,\nNOAA\n9, and\nNOAA\n10 spacecraft were simultaneously\noperational.\nTh.is paper covers normal\nand special operations\nof the spacecraft and instruments,\noperational\nanomalies,\nand the _,:sponses of thee in.s\'truments\nto in-orbit\nand scasorml variations\nin the\n,solar cT_viro77nlent.\n\nIntroduction\nThe objective\nof the Earth Radiation\nBudget\nExperiment\n(ERBE)\nis to deduce\nlong-tern_\ntrends\nin\nmonthly\naverages\nof the Earth\'s\nlongwave\nand shortwave radiation\nfields.\nTo accomplish\nthis objective,\nERBE\ninstruments\nwere launched\ninto Earth\norbits\naboard\nthe Earth Radiation\nBudget Satellite\n(ERBS)\n(operated\nt).,,, NASA)\nin October\n1984 and aboard\nthe NOAA\n9 and NOAA\n10 spacecraft\n(operated\nby the National\nOceanic\nand Atmospheric\nAdministration)\nin December\n1984 and September\n1986,\nrespectively.\nValidation\naim archival\nof data from\nthe first. 15 months\nof instrmnent\noperation,\nNow\'mbet 1984 through\nJanuary\n1986, were completed\nin\nMarch\n1990. Reference\n1 describes\nmission\nstrategy\nand operation\nof the ERBE\ninstrmnents\naboard\nthe\nERBS and NOAA spacecraft\nduring\nthat\n15-month\nperiod.\nReference\n1 also gives the overview\nof the\nERBE\ninission,\nthe design\nand operational\nfeatures\nof the ERBE\ninstruments,\nand a description\nof the\nERBE science data processing.\nValidation\n\nand archival\n\nof data\n\nfrom the\n\nERBE\n\nin-\n\nstruments\nfor the period from February\n1986 through\nJanuary\n1987 were completed\nin July 1991.\nFrom\nFebruary\n1, 1986,\nuntil\nOctober\n24, 1986,\ndata\nare available\nonly from the instruments\naboard\nthe\nERBS\nand NOAA\n9 spacecraft.\nOn October\n24\nboth instruments\naboard\nthe NOAA\n10 spacecraft\nbecame\noperational.\nThus\nbegan\na period\nduring\nwhich ERBE instruments\nwere operational\noil. ERBS,\nNOAA\n9, and NOAA\n10.\nThe overlap\nperiod\nfor\nmeasurements\nfrom the three scanners\nwas cut short\n\nby the failure\nof the scanner\ninstrument\non the\nNOAA\n9 spacecraft\non Jammry\n20, 1987.\nThe period of overlap\nof scanner\ndata was further\nshortened\nby operational\nproblems\nwith the scanner\ninstrument\non the NOAA\n10 spacecraft\nduring\nNovember\nand\nDecember\n1986.\nThis paper\ndescribes\nthe in-orbit\noperation\nof\nthe\nERBE\ninstrunwnts\nduring\ntheir\nsecond\nfllll\nyear\nof operat.ion,\nfrom\nFebruary\n1986\nthrough\nJammry\n1987. Degnan,\n\n4;/\n\n(Maximum\n\n200 words)\n\nInstrmlmnts\nof the Earth\nRadiation\nBudget\nExt)eriment\n(ERBE)\nare operating\non three different\nEarth-orbiting\nspacecraft.\nThe Earth\nRadiation\nBudget\nSatellite\n(ERBS)\nis operated\nby the Natitlnal\nAeronautics\nand Space\nAdministration\n(NASA),\nand the NOAA\n9 and NOAA\nl0 weather\nsatellites\nare operated\nI)y the National\nOceanic\nand Atinospheric\nAdministratioll\n(NOAA).\nThis\npaper\nis the second\nin a series that describes\nthe\nERBE\nmission,\nin-orbit\nenvironments,\ninstrument\ndesign\nand operati(mal\nfeatures,\nand data processing\nand\nvalidation\nprocedures.\nThis paper\ndecribes\nthe spacecraft\nand instrmnenI\noperations\nfor tile second\nf_fll year\nof in-orbit\noperations,\nwhich extends\nfrom February\n1986 through\nJanuary\n1987. Validation\nand archival\nof\nradiation\nmeasurements\nmade by ERBE\ninstruments\nduring\nthis second\nyear of operation\nwere COnlpiet.ed in\nJuly 1991. This period\nincludes\nthe only time, November\n1986 through\n.lanuary\n1987, during\nwhich all ERBE\ninstrmnents\naboard\nthe ERBS,\nNOAA\n9, and NOAA\n10 spacecraft\nwere simultaneously\noperatiomd,\nThe\npaper covers\nnormal\nand special\noperations\nof the spacecraft\nand ii[st.ruments,\noperational\nanomalies,\nand the\nresponses\nof the inst_rmnents\nto in-orbit\nand seasonal\nvariations\nin tile solar environment.\n\n14.\n\nSUBJECT\n\nERBE;\n\n1S.\n\nTERMS\n\nERBS;\n\nInstrument\n\noperations\',\n\nMission\n\nanalysis;\n\nOrbital\n\nNUMBER\n\nOF\n\nPAGES\n\n215\n\nenvironment\n16.\n\nPRICE\n\nCODE\n\nAI0\n17.\n\nSECURITY\nOF\n\nCLASSIFICATION\n\nREPORT\n\nUnclassified\nSN\n\n7540-01-280-5S00\n\n18.\n\nSECURITY\nOF\n\nTHIS\n\nCLASSIFICATIOf_\nPAGE\n\nlg.\n\nSECURITY\nOF\n\nCLASSIFICATION\n\nABSTRACT\n\n20.
